- [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-104">.NET framework 4.7.2</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-104">.NET Framework 4.7.2</span></span>](#v472)

- [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-108">.NET framework 4.6.1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-108">.NET Framework 4.6.1</span></span>](#v461)

- [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-112">.NET Framework 4.5</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-112">.NET Framework 4.5</span></span>](#v45)

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-113">Bu makale, her yeni özellik hakkında kapsamlı bilgi sağlamaz ve değiştirilebilir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-113">This article does not provide comprehensive information about each new feature and is subject to change.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-114">.NET Framework hakkında genel bilgi için bkz. > [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-117">.NET Framwork takımındaki özellikleri ile NuGet platform desteğini artırmak ve değişmez koleksiyonlar ve SIMD etkin vektör türlerinin gibi yeni işlevleri tanıtmak için bant dışı da serbest bırakır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-117">The .NET Framework team also releases features out of band with NuGet to expand platform support and to introduce new functionality, such as immutable collections and SIMD-enabled vector types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-118">Daha fazla bilgi için [ek sınıf kitaplıkları ve API'ler](../additional-apis/index.md) ve [.NET Framework ve bant dışı yayınlar](~/docs/framework/get-started/the-net-framework-and-out-of-band-releases.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-118">For more information, see [Additional Class Libraries and APIs](../additional-apis/index.md) and [The .NET Framework and Out-of-Band Releases](~/docs/framework/get-started/the-net-framework-and-out-of-band-releases.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-119">Bkz: bir [NuGet paketlerini tam listesi](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/p/nugetpackages/) .NET Framework veya abone [veri akışımıza](https://nuget.org/api/v2/curated-feeds/dotnetframework/Packages/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-119">See a [complete list of NuGet packages](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/p/nugetpackages/) for the .NET Framework, or subscribe to [our feed](https://nuget.org/api/v2/curated-feeds/dotnetframework/Packages/).</span></span>

<a name="v472" />

## <a name="introducing-the-net-framework-472"></a><span data-ttu-id="3c992-120">.NET Framework 4.7.2 ile tanışın</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-120">Introducing the .NET Framework 4.7.2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-121">.NET Framework'ün önceki sürümlerinde .NET Framework 4.7.2 yapılar çok kararlı bir ürüne kalan sırasında birçok yeni düzeltmeyi ve çeşitli yeni özellikler ekleyerek 4.x.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-121">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 builds on previous versions of the .NET Framework 4.x by adding many new fixes and several new features while remaining a very stable product.</span></span>

### <a name="downloading-and-installing-the-net-framework-472"></a><span data-ttu-id="3c992-122">.NET Framework'ü 4.7.2 yükleme ve indirme</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-122">Downloading and installing the .NET Framework 4.7.2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-123">.NET Framework 4.7.2 aşağıdaki konumlardan indirebilirsiniz:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-123">You can download the .NET Framework 4.7.2  from the following locations:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-124">.NET framework 4.7.2 Web yükleyicisi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-124">.NET Framework 4.7.2 Web Installer</span></span>](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=863262)

- [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-125">NET Framework 4.7.2 çevrimdışı yükleyici</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-125">NET Framework 4.7.2 Offline Installer</span></span>](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=863265)

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-126">.NET Framework 4.7.2 Windows 10, Windows 8.1, Windows 7 SP1 ve Windows Server 2008 R2 SP1 ile başlayarak, karşılık gelen sunucu platformları yüklenebilir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-126">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 can be installed on Windows 10, Windows 8.1, Windows 7 SP1, and the corresponding server platforms starting with Windows Server 2008 R2 SP1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-127">Web yükleyicisini veya çevrimdışı yükleyiciyi kullanarak .NET Framework 4.7.2 yükleyebilirsiniz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-127">You can install the .NET Framework 4.7.2 by using either the web installer or the offline installer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-128">Çoğu kullanıcı için önerilen yol, web yükleyicisi kullanmaktır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-128">The recommended way for most users is to use the web installer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-129">.NET Framework 4.7.2 Visual Studio 2012 veya daha sonra yükleyerek hedefleyebilir [4.7.2 .NET Framework Geliştirici paketi](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=874338).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-129">You can target the .NET Framework 4.7.2 in Visual Studio 2012 or later by installing the [.NET Framework 4.7.2 Developer Pack](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/?LinkId=874338).</span></span>

### <a name="whats-new-in-the-net-framework-472"></a><span data-ttu-id="3c992-130">4.7.2 .NET Framework'teki yenilikler</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-130">What's new in the .NET Framework 4.7.2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-131">.NET Framework 4.7.2 aşağıdaki alanlarda yeni özellikler içerir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-131">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 includes new features in the following areas:</span></span>

- [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-132">Çekirdek</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-132">Core</span></span>](#core-472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-133">ASP.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-133">ASP.NET</span></span>](#asp-net472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-134">Ağ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-134">Networking</span></span>](#net472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-135">SQL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-135">SQL</span></span>](#sql472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-136">WPF</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-136">WPF</span></span>](#wpf472)
- [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-137">ClickOnce</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-137">ClickOnce</span></span>](#clickonce)

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-138">.NET Framework'teki 4.7.2 devam eden bir odak yardımcı teknoloji kullanıcılar için uygun bir deneyim sağlamak için uygulamanın veren geliştirilmiş erişilebilirlik olur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-138">A continuing focus in the .NET Framework 4.7.2 is improved accessibility, which allows an application to provide an appropriate experience for users of Assistive Technology.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-139">.NET Framework'teki 4.7.2 erişilebilirlik geliştirme hakkında daha fazla bilgi için bkz: [erişilebilirlik .NET Framework'teki yenilikler](whats-new-in-accessibility.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-139">For information on accessibility improvement in the .NET Framework 4.7.2, see [What's new in accessibility in the .NET Framework](whats-new-in-accessibility.md).</span></span>

<a name="core-472" />

#### <a name="core"></a><span data-ttu-id="3c992-140">Çekirdek</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-140">Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-141">.NET Framework 4.7.2 çok sayıda şifreleme geliştirmelerinden, ZIP arşivlerini ve ek koleksiyon API'leri daha iyi sıkıştırma desteği sunar.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-141">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 features a large number of cryptographic enhancements, better decompression support for ZIP archives, and additional collection APIs.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-142">**RSA yeni aşırı yüklemeleri. Oluşturma ve DSA. Oluşturma**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-142">**New overloads of RSA.Create and DSA.Create**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-143"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.DSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> Ve <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.RSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> yöntemleri, yeni bir örnek oluşturulduğunda anahtar parametreleri sağlamanıza olanak tanır <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> veya <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> anahtarı.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-143">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.DSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Security.Cryptography.RSAParameters)?displayProperty=nameWithType> methods let you supply key parameters when instantiated a new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> or <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> key.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-144">Kod aşağıdaki gibi değiştirin olanak sağlar:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-144">They allow you to replace code like the following:</span></span>

```csharp
// Before .NET Framework 4.7.2
using (RSA rsa = RSA.Create())
{
   rsa.ImportParameters(rsaParameters);
   // Other code to execute using the RSA instance.
}
```

```vb
' Before .NET Framework 4.7.2
Using rsa = RSA.Create()
   rsa.ImportParameters(rsaParameters)
   ' Other code to execute using the rsa instance.
End Using
```
<span data-ttu-id="3c992-145">şunun gibi kod ile:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-145">with code like this:</span></span>
```csharp
// Starting with .NET Framework 4.7.2
using (RSA rsa = RSA.Create(rsaParameters))
{
   // Other code to execute using the rsa instance.
}
```
```vb
' Starting with .NET Framework 4.7.2
Using rsa = RSA.Create(rsaParameters)
   ' Other code to execute using the rsa instance.
End Using
```

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-146"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> Ve <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> yöntemleri yeni oluşturmanıza izin <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> veya <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> belirli bir anahtar boyutu anahtarı.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-146">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> and <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA.Create(System.Int32)?displayProperty=nameWithType> methods let you generate new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.DSA> or <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.RSA> keys with a specific key size.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-147">Örneğin:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-147">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
using (DSA dsa = DSA.Create(2048))
{
   // Other code to execute using the dsa instance.
}
```
```vb
Using dsa = DSA.Create(2048)
   ' Other code to execute using the dsa instance.
End Using
```

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-148">**Rfc2898DeriveBytes oluşturucular bir karma algoritması adı kabul edin.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-148">**Rfc2898DeriveBytes constructors accept a hash algorithm name**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-149"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Rfc2898DeriveBytes> Sınıfında üç yeni oluşturucularla bir <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.HashAlgorithmName> anahtarları türetilirken kullanılacak HMAC algoritmasını tanımlar parametresi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-149">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Rfc2898DeriveBytes> class has three new constructors with a <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.HashAlgorithmName> parameter that identifies the HMAC algorithm to use when deriving keys.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-150">SHA-1 kullanmak yerine, geliştiriciler gibi SHA-256, SHA-2 tabanlı bir HMAC aşağıdaki örnekte gösterildiği gibi kullanmanız gerekir:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-150">Instead of using SHA-1, developers should use a SHA-2-based HMAC like SHA-256, as shown in the following example:</span></span>

```csharp
private static byte[] DeriveKey(string password, out int iterations, out byte[] salt,
                                out HashAlgorithmName algorithm)
{
   iterations = 100000;
   algorithm = HashAlgorithmName.SHA256;

   const int SaltSize = 32;
   const int DerivedValueSize = 32;

   using (Rfc2898DeriveBytes pbkdf2 = new Rfc2898DeriveBytes(password, SaltSize,
                                                             iterations, algorithm))
   {
      salt = pbkdf2.Salt;
      return pbkdf2.GetBytes(DerivedValueSize);
   }
}
```
```vb
Private Shared Function DeriveKey(password As String, ByRef iterations As Integer,
                                  ByRef salt AS Byte(), ByRef algorithm As HashAlgorithmName) As Byte()
   iterations = 100000
   algorithm = HashAlgorithmName.SHA256

   Const SaltSize As Integer = 32
   Const  DerivedValueSize As Integer = 32

   Using pbkdf2 = New Rfc2898DeriveBytes(password, SaltSize, iterations, algorithm)
      salt = pbkdf2.Salt
      Return pbkdf2.GetBytes(DerivedValueSize)
   End Using
End Function
```

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-151">**Kısa ömürlü anahtarlar için destek**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-151">**Support for ephemeral keys**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-152">PFX alma, özel anahtarları isteğe bağlı olarak sabit sürücüyü atlayarak bellekten doğrudan yükleyebilirsiniz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-152">PFX import can optionally load private keys directly from memory, bypassing the hard drive.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="3c992-153"> Zaman yeni <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509KeyStorageFlags.EphemeralKeySet?displayProperty=nameWithType> bayrağı belirtilen bir <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2> oluşturucu veya aşırı yüklemelerinden birini <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.Import%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> yöntemi özel anahtarlar kısa ömürlü anahtarlar olarak yüklenir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-153"> When the new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509KeyStorageFlags.EphemeralKeySet?displayProperty=nameWithType> flag is specified in an <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2> constructor or one of the overloads of the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.Import%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> method, the private keys will be loaded as ephemeral keys.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-154">Bu anahtarları diskte görünür olmasını önler.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-154">This prevents the keys from being visible on the disk.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-155">Ancak:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-155">However:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3c992-156">Disk için sertifikalar ile yüklenen anahtarları sürdürülmeyen olduğundan bu bayrağı için bir X509Store eklemek için iyi adaylar değildir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-156">Since the keys are not persisted to disk, certificates loaded with this flag are not good candidates to add to an X509Store.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3c992-157">Bu şekilde yüklenen anahtarları, neredeyse her zaman Windows CNG yüklenir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-157">Keys loaded in this manner are almost always loaded via Windows CNG.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-158">Bu nedenle, Arayanların özel anahtarı genişletme yöntemleri çağırarak erişmesi gereken [sertifika. GetRSAPrivateKey()](xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.RSACertificateExtensions.GetRSAPrivateKey%2A).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-158">Therefore, callers must access the private key by calling extension methods, such as [cert.GetRSAPrivateKey()](xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.RSACertificateExtensions.GetRSAPrivateKey%2A).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-159"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> Özelliği çalışmaz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-159">The <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> property does not function.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3c992-160">Eski beri <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> özelliği sertifikalarla çalışmıyor, geliştiriciler için kısa ömürlü anahtarlar geçmeden önce sıkı testlerden gerçekleştirmesi gereken.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-160">Since the legacy <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.X509Certificates.X509Certificate2.PrivateKey?displayProperty=nameWithType> property does not work with certificates, developers should perform rigorous testing before switching to ephemeral keys.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-161">**PKCS #10 sertifika imzalama isteği X.509 ortak anahtar sertifikaları ve program oluşturma**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-161">**Programmatic creation of PKCS#10 certification signing requests and X.509 public key certificates**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-162">.NET Framework 4.7.2 ile başlayarak, iş yüklerini olanak sağlayan araçları içine aşamalandırılacak sertifika isteği oluşturma isteği (CSR) imzalama sertifikası oluşturabilirsiniz.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-162">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, workloads can generate certificate signing requests (CSRs), which allows certificate request generation to be staged into existing tooling.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-163">Bu, sık test senaryolarda yararlıdır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-163">This is frequently useful in test scenarios.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-164">Daha fazla bilgi ve kod örnekleri için bkz. "programlı oluşturulmasını PKCS #10 sertifika imzalama istekleri ve ortak anahtar sertifikaları X.509" içinde [.NET Blog](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2018/03/08/net-framework-4-7-2-developer-pack-early-access-build-3056-is-available/).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-164">For more information and code examples, see "Programmatic creation of PKCS#10 certification signing requests and X.509 public key certificates" in the [.NET Blog](https://blogs.msdn.microsoft.com/dotnet/2018/03/08/net-framework-4-7-2-developer-pack-early-access-build-3056-is-available/).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-165">**Yeni SignerInfo üyeler**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-165">**New SignerInfo members**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-166">4.7.2, .NET Framework ile başlayarak <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo> sınıfı imza hakkında daha fazla bilgi gösterir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-166">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo> class exposes more information about the signature.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-167">Değerini alabilir <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.SignatureAlgorithm?displayProperty=fullName> imzalayan tarafından kullanılan imza algoritmasını belirlemek için özellik.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-167">You can retrieve the value of the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.SignatureAlgorithm?displayProperty=fullName> property to determine the signature algorithm used by the signer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-168"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.GetSignature%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> Bu imzalayan için şifreleme imzası bir kopyasını almak için çağrılabilir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-168"><xref:System.Security.Cryptography.Pkcs.SignerInfo.GetSignature%2A?displayProperty=nameWithType> can be called to get a copy of the cryptographic signature for this signer.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-169">**Sarmalanan bir akış CryptoStream bırakıldıktan sonra açık bırakın**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-169">**Leaving a wrapped stream open after CryptoStream is disposed**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-170">4.7.2, .NET Framework ile başlayarak <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> sınıfında sağlayan ek bir Oluşturucuda <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream.Dispose%2A> Sarmalanan akış kapatmadığınızdan.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-170">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> class has an additional constructor that allows <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream.Dispose%2A> to not close the wrapped stream.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="3c992-171"> Sarmalanan akış sonra açık bırakmak <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> örneği kullanıldığında, yeni bir çağrı <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> Oluşturucu aşağıdaki gibi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-171"> To leave the wrapped stream open after the <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> instance is disposed, call the new <xref:System.Security.Cryptography.CryptoStream> constructor as follows:</span></span>

```csharp
var cStream = new CryptoStream(stream, transform, mode, leaveOpen: true);
```
```vb
Dim cStream = New CryptoStream(stream, transform, mode, leaveOpen:=true)
```

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-172">**DeflateStream açma değişiklikleri**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-172">**Decompression changes in DeflateStream**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-173">4.7.2, .NET Framework uygulamasını açma işlemlerinde başlayarak <xref:System.IO.Compression.DeflateStream> sınıfı, varsayılan olarak yerel Windows API'ları kullanacak şekilde değiştirildi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-173">Starting with the .NET Framework 4.7.2, the implementation of decompression operations in the <xref:System.IO.Compression.DeflateStream> class has changed to use native Windows APIs by default.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-174">Genellikle, bu önemli performans geliştirmeyle sonuçlanır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-174">Typically, this results in a substantial performance improvement.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-175">Windows API'leri kullanarak açma desteği, .NET Framework 4.7.2 hedefleyen uygulamalar için varsayılan olarak etkindir.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-175">Support for decompression by using Windows APIs is enabled by default for applications that target .NET Framework 4.7.2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-176">.NET Framework'ün önceki sürümlerini hedefleyen ancak .NET Framework 4.7.2 altında çalışan uygulamalar özelliğini bu davranışı aşağıdakileri ekleyerek [AppContext anahtar](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/appcontextswitchoverrides-element.md) için uygulama yapılandırma dosyası:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-176">Applications that target earlier versions of .NET Framework but are running under .NET Framework 4.7.2 can opt into this behavior by adding the following [AppContext switch](../configure-apps/file-schema/runtime/appcontextswitchoverrides-element.md) to the application configuration file:</span></span>

```xml
<AppContextSwitchOverrides value="Switch.System.IO.Compression.DoNotUseNativeZipLibraryForDecompression=false" />
```

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-177">**Ek koleksiyon API'leri**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-177">**Additional collection APIs**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-178">Bir dizi yeni API için .NET Framework 4.7.2 ekler <xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601> ve <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> türleri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-178">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 adds a number of new APIs to the <xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601> and <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-179">Bu güncelleştirmeler şunlardır:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-179">These include:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3c992-180">`TryGetValue` Bu iki tür diğer koleksiyon türlerine kullanılan deneyin deseni genişletme yöntemleri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-180">`TryGetValue` methods, which extend the try pattern used in other collection types to these two types.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-181">Yöntemler şunlardır:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-181">The methods are:</span></span>

   - [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-182">Genel bool HashSet<T>. TryGetValue (T actualValue kullanıma T equalValue)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-182">public bool HashSet<T>.TryGetValue(T equalValue, out T actualValue)</span></span>](xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601.TryGetValue%2A)
   - [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-183">Genel bool SortedSet<T>. TryGetValue (T actualValue kullanıma T equalValue)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-183">public bool SortedSet<T>.TryGetValue(T equalValue, out T actualValue)</span></span>](xref:System.Collections.Generic.SortedSet%601.TryGetValue%2A)

- <span data-ttu-id="3c992-184">`Enumerable.To*` bir koleksiyona Dönüştür genişletme yöntemleri, bir <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601>:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-184">`Enumerable.To*` extension methods, which convert a collection to a <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601>:</span></span>

   - [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-185">Genel statik HashSet<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(Bu IEnumerable<TSource> kaynak)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-185">public static HashSet<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(this IEnumerable<TSource> source)</span></span>](xref:System.Linq.Enumerable.ToHashSet%2A)
   - [<span data-ttu-id="3c992-186">Genel statik HashSet<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(Bu IEnumerable<TSource> kaynak IEqualityComparer<TSource> karşılaştırıcı)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-186">public static HashSet<TSource> ToHashSet<TSource>(this IEnumerable<TSource> source, IEqualityComparer<TSource> comparer)</span></span>](xref:System.Linq.Enumerable.ToHashSet%2A)

- <span data-ttu-id="3c992-187">Yeni <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> olanak tanıyan oluşturucular bir performans kazancı boyutunu bildiğinizde veren koleksiyonun kapasitesi ayarlama <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> önceden:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-187">New <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> constructors that let you set the collection's capacity, which yields a performance benefit when you know the size of the <xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601> in advance:</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="3c992-188">[Genel HashSet (int Kapasite)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-188">[public HashSet(int capacity)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32))</span></span>
   - <span data-ttu-id="3c992-189">[Genel HashSet (int kapasite IEqualityComparer<T> karşılaştırıcı)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32,System.Collections.Generic.IEqualityComparer%7B%600%7D))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-189">[public HashSet(int capacity, IEqualityComparer<T> comparer)](xref:System.Collections.Generic.HashSet%601.%23ctor(System.Int32,System.Collections.Generic.IEqualityComparer%7B%600%7D))</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-190"><xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602> Sınıfı içeren yeni aşırı yüklemeleri <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.AddOrUpdate%2A> ve <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.GetOrAdd%2A> yöntemleri sözlükten bir değer almak veya değil bulunursa ve eklemek için sözlük veya zaten varsa güncelleştirmek için bir değer ekleyin.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-190">The <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602> class includes new overloads of the <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.AddOrUpdate%2A> and <xref:System.Collections.Concurrent.ConcurrentDictionary%602.GetOrAdd%2A> methods to retrieve a value from the dictionary or to add it if it is not found, and to add a value to the dictionary or to update it if it already exists.</span></span>

```csharp
public TValue AddOrUpdate<TArg>(TKey key, Func<TKey, TArg, TValue> addValueFactory, Func<TKey, TValue, TArg, TValue> updateValueFactory, TArg factoryArgument)

public TValue GetOrAdd<TArg>(TKey key, Func<TKey, TArg, TValue> valueFactory, TArg factoryArgument)
```

```vb
Public AddOrUpdate(Of TArg)(key As TKey, addValueFactory As Func(Of TKey, TArg, TValue), updateValueFactory As Func(Of TKey, TValue, TArg, TValue), factoryArgument As TArg) As TValue

Public GetOrAdd(Of TArg)(key As TKey, valueFactory As Func(Of TKey, TArg, TValue), factoryArgument As TArg) As TValue
```

#### <a name="aspnet"></a><span data-ttu-id="3c992-191">ASP.NET</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-191">ASP.NET</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-192">**Web Forms bağımlılık ekleme desteği**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-192">**Support for dependency injection in Web Forms**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-193">[Bağımlılık ekleme (dı)](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/dependency-injection#overview-of-dependency-injection) böylece nesnenin kod artık yalnızca bir bağımlılık değiştiği için değiştirilmesi gereken nesneleri ve bunların bağımlılıklarını ayırır.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-193">[Dependency injection (DI)](/aspnet/core/fundamentals/dependency-injection#overview-of-dependency-injection) decouples objects and their dependencies so that an object's code no longer needs to be changed just because a dependency has changed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-194">.NET Framework'ü 4.7.2 hedefleyen ASP.NET uygulamaları geliştirirken, aşağıdakileri yapabilirsiniz:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-194">When developing ASP.NET applications that target the .NET Framework 4.7.2, you can:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3c992-195">Ayarlayıcı, arabirimi ve oluşturucu tabanlı yerleştirmeye kullanın [işleyicileri ve modülleri](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/aspnet/bb398986(v=vs.100)), [sayfasında örnekleri](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), ve [kullanıcı denetimleri](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/aspnet/y6wb1a0e(v=vs.100)) ASP.NET web uygulaması projeleri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-195">Use setter-based, interface-based, and constructor-based injection in [handlers and modules](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/aspnet/bb398986(v=vs.100)), [Page instances](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), and [user controls](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/aspnet/y6wb1a0e(v=vs.100)) of ASP.NET web application projects.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3c992-196">Ayarlayıcı ve arabirim tabanlı yerleştirmeye kullanın [işleyicileri ve modülleri](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/aspnet/bb398986(v=vs.100)), [sayfasında örnekleri](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), ve [kullanıcı denetimleri](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/aspnet/y6wb1a0e(v=vs.100)) ASP.NET web sitesi projeleri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-196">Use setter-based and interface-based injection in [handlers and modules](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/aspnet/bb398986(v=vs.100)), [Page instances](xref:System.Web.UI.Page), and [user controls](https://docs.microsoft.com/previous-versions/aspnet/y6wb1a0e(v=vs.100)) of ASP.NET web site projects.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="3c992-197">Farklı bağımlılık ekleme çerçeveleri takın.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-197">Plug in different dependency injection frameworks.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-198">**Aynı sitede tanımlama bilgileri için destek**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-198">**Support for same-site cookies**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-199">[SameSite](https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-west-first-party-cookies-07) bir tarayıcı siteler arası istek birlikte bir tanımlama bilgisi göndermesini engeller.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-199">[SameSite](https://tools.ietf.org/html/draft-west-first-party-cookies-07) prevents a browser from sending a cookie along with a cross-site request.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-200">.NET Framework 4.7.2 ekler bir <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie.SameSite?displayProperty=nameWithType> özellik değeri olan bir <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode?displayProperty=nameWithType> numaralandırma üyesi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-200">The .NET Framework 4.7.2 adds a <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie.SameSite?displayProperty=nameWithType> property whose value is a <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode?displayProperty=nameWithType> enumeration member.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-201">Öğenin değeri ise <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Strict?displayProperty=nameWithType> veya <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Lax?displayProperty=nameWithType>, ASP.NET ekler `SameSite` özniteliği için set-cookie üstbilgisi.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-201">If its value is <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Strict?displayProperty=nameWithType> or <xref:System.Web.SameSiteMode.Lax?displayProperty=nameWithType>, ASP.NET adds the `SameSite` attribute to the set-cookie header.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="3c992-202">SameSite destek uygulandığı <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> , de olarak nesneleri için <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> ve <xref:System.Web.SessionState> tanımlama bilgileri.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-202">SameSite support applies to <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> objects, as well as to <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> and <xref:System.Web.SessionState> cookies.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="3c992-203">SameSite için ayarlayabileceğiniz bir <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> gibi nesnesi:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-203">You can set SameSite for an <xref:System.Web.HttpCookie> object as follows:</span></span>

```csharp
var c = new HttpCookie("secureCookie", "same origin");
c.SameSite = SameSiteMode.Lax;
```
```vb
Dim c As New HttpCookie("secureCookie", "same origin")
c.SameSite = SameSiteMode.Lax
```
<span data-ttu-id="3c992-204">Web.config dosyasını değiştirerek SameSite tanımlama bilgileri uygulama düzeyinde de yapılandırabilirsiniz:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-204">You can also configure SameSite cookies at the application level by modifying the web.config file:</span></span>

```xml
<system.web>
   <httpCookies sameSite="Strict" />
</system.web>
```
<span data-ttu-id="3c992-205">SameSite için ekleyebilirsiniz <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> ve <xref:System.Web.SessionState> web yapılandırma dosyasını değiştirerek tanımlama bilgileri:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="3c992-205">You can add SameSite for <xref:System.Web.Security.FormsAuthentication> and <xref:System.Web.SessionState> cookies by modifying the web config file:</span></span>

```xml
<system.web>
   <authentication mode="Forms">
      <forms cookieSameSite="Lax">
         <!-- ...   -->
      </forms>
   <authentication />
   <sessionSate cookieSameSite="Lax"></sessionState>
</system.web>
```
